AajurroomiyyahChapter2=Na te ihoparau|kei te mohio|ki tino,|ka kite,|a ka,|me te taa|o te wahinetanga|oro-iti.|te matūriki|reira|e kore|e manako|ki reira|tohu|o te kupu ingoa|a kihai|tohu|o te kupu ingoa.|te tatau|o te kōpapa|kōpapa|Ko reira:|taui te reira|nga hopearaa|o nga kupu|i te rerekētanga|o te kaha huānga / Regent|tomo|ki runga ki taua mea|kitea|rānei|feruri.|Na ona wahi|e wha:|take nominative,|me te take accusative,|me te take pūriro,|a jussive / take matahao,|Na hoki tūingoa|mai i|e|take nominative,|me te take accusative,|me te take pūriro,|a kihai|take jussive / hōtiu|i roto i reira,|Na hoki tūmahi|mai i|e|take nominative,|me te take accusative,|a jussive / take matahao,|a kihai|take pānga|i roto i reira.
AajurroomiyyahChapter3=Ūpoko ! !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!|tuatahi|tohu|o te kōpapa / take mutu|Hoki te take nominative|ki roto|Whā|tohu:|te damma,|me te matenui,|me te alef,|me te poutumarotanga.|Na ka hoki|te damma|Na ko reira|tohu|hoki te take nominative|ki roto|Whā|tūranga:|te kupu ingoa|puka kotahi,|me te takitini|whati,|me te takitini|wahine|tangi,|me te ihoparau|hakari|e|kahore e|piri / whakapā|me tona mutunga|Aha noa|A hoki|te matenui|na ko|tohu|hoki te take nominative|ki roto|e rua ngā take:|ki roto|te vahine|tautāne|tangi,|a i roto i|nga tūingoa|e rima,|a ko ratou:|tou papa,|ko to koutou teina,|me to koutou papa-i roto i-ture,|ko koutou mangai,|me e tangohia|o te taonga.|A hoki|te alef|na ko|tohu|hoki te take nominative|ki roto|rua|tūingoa|rawa.
AajurroomiyyahChapter4=A hoki|te poutumarotanga|na ko|tohu|hoki te take nominative|ki roto|te ihoparau|hakari,|ka|Kua Āpitihia|ki reira|tūpou|o whene,|rānei|tūpou|o plurality,|rānei|tūpou|o te wahinetanga|whakatutuki / tangata tuarua.|A mo te take accusative|e rima|tohu|te fatha,|me te alef,|me te kasra,|me te a Ihowa,|me te mukunga|o te poutumarotanga.|Na ka hoki|te fatha|na ko|he tohu|mo te take accusative|ki roto|e toru|take:|ki roto|te kupu ingoa|te motuhia e,|a te vahine|whati,|me te ihoparau|hakari kukū|ka|tomo|ki reira|te take subjunctive,|a kahore e|Kua Āpitihia|me tona mutunga|Aha noa|A hoki|te alef|na ko|he tohu|hoki accusative|ki roto|nga tūingoa|e rima,|rite tika:|(Kite ahau|tou papa|me to koutou teina)|a he aha|rite|e.
AajurroomiyyahChapter5=A hoki|te kasra|na ko|he tohu|hoki te take accusative|ki roto|te vahine|wahine|tangi.|A hoki|te a Ihowa|na ko|he tohu|hoki te take accusative|ki roto|te rua|me te takitini.|A hoki|te mukunga|o te poutumarotanga|na ko|he tohu|mo te take accusative|ki roto|nga tūmahi|e rima|e|tona take nominative|ki te tamau|o te poutumarotanga.|A mo te take pūriro|e toru|tohu:|te kasra,|me te a Ihowa,|me te fatha.|Na ka hoki|te kasra|na ko|he tohu|hoki te take pūriro|ki roto|e toru|take:|ki roto|te kupu ingoa|motuhia|tino inflected,|a te vahine|whati|tino inflected,|a i roto i|te vahine|o te wahinetanga|tangi.|A hoki|te a Ihowa|na ko|he tohu|hoki te take pūriro|ki roto|e toru|take:|ki roto|nga tūingoa|e rima,|a i roto i|whene|me te vahine rau.
AajurroomiyyahChapter6=A hoki|te fatha|na ko|he tohu|hoki te take pūriro|ki roto|te kupu ingoa|e|e kore|tino inflected.|A mo te take jussive|rua tohu:|te sukun,|me te mukunga.|Na ka hoki|te sukun|Na ko reira|te tohu|hoki te take jussive|ki roto|te ihoparau|hakari|tangi|mutu.|A hoki|te mukunga|ko reira|he tohu|hoki jussive|ki roto|te ihoparau|hakari|ngoikore|o mutu|a i roto i|nga tūmahi|e rima|e|ona tohu|ki te tango|o te poutumarotanga.|Wehenga|o te inflected|te inflected|e rua nga wahi:|he wahi|inflected|ki nga tohu oropuare,|me te wahi|inflected|ki pukapuka.
AajurroomiyyahChapter7=Na e|inflected|ki nga tohu oro|Whā|mea:|te kupu ingoa|te motuhia e,|me te takitini|o te maru,|me te takitini|o wahine|tangi,|me te ihoparau|hakari kukū|e|e kore|kua tūhono;connected|me tona mutunga|Aha noa|A ia o ratou|nominative hanga|ki damma,|ka hanga accusative|ki fatha,|ka hanga pūriro|ki kasra,|ka hanga jussive|ki sukun,|ka wehea|mai i|e|e toru|mea:|te takitini|o te wahinetanga|tangi|hanga accusative|ki kasra,|me te kupu ingoa|e|e kore|tino inflectable|Kei te hanga pūriro|ki fatha,|me te ihoparau|hakari|Kua Āpitihia|tona mutunga|jussive|ki te mukua|o ona mutunga.|A i|inflects|ki pukapuka|e wha|momo:|te rua,|me te takitini|o te tamatane|tangi,|me nga tūingoa|e rima,|me nga tūmahi|e rima,|a ko ratou:|ratou e rua tautāne mahi,|a ratou rua wahine / koutou mahi e rua|ratou tautāne katoa mahi,|koe tautāne katoa te mahi,|me te wahine koe mahi.
